##################################################
namespace = luxevents

#oldman visit
character_event = {
	id = 554350001
	desc = "EVTDESC554350001"
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

    is_triggered_only = yes	
	
	only_playable = yes
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	ai = no

	trigger = {
		
		NOT = { has_character_flag = flavor_event_1 }
		in_command = no
		NOT = { trait = on_hajj }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = flavor_event_1
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA554350001"
		change_learning = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB554350001"
		change_martial = 1
	}
}

#thief1
character_event = {
	id = 554350007
	desc = "EVTDESC554350007"
	picture = GFX_evt_market

    is_triggered_only = yes	
	
	only_playable = yes
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	ai = no

	trigger = {
			
		NOT = { has_character_flag = flavor_event_7 }	
		in_command = no
		NOT = { 
			OR = {
				trait = brave
				trait = wounded
				trait = craven
				trait = deceitful
				trait = on_hajj
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = flavor_event_7
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA554350007"	
		random_list = {
			50 = { 
				add_trait = brave
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38270
					}
				}
			}
			50 = { 
 				add_trait = wounded
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38280
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB554350007"
		random_list = {
			50 = { 
 				add_trait = craven
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38257
					}
				}
			}
			50 = { 
 				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#priest3
character_event = {
	id = 554350018
	desc = "EVTDESC554350018"
	picture = GFX_evt_royalcourt

    is_triggered_only = yes	
	
	only_playable = yes
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	ai = no

	trigger = {
			
		NOT = { has_character_flag = flavor_event_18 }	
		in_command = no
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				trait = on_hajj
				trait = zealous
				trait = cynical
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = flavor_event_18
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA554350018"	
		set_character_flag = flag_duel_to_the_death
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		trigger = {
			any_courtier = {
				age = 16
				prisoner = no
				NOT = {
					trait = incapable
				}
				OR = {
					is_female = no
					trait = master_warrior
				}
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				age = 16
				prisoner = no
				NOT = {
					trait = incapable
				}
				OR = {
					is_female = no
					trait = master_warrior
				}
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
			character_event = {
				id = lux_duels.1
				tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPlux_duels.1"
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA554350018"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_courtier = {
					age = 16
					prisoner = no
					NOT = {
						trait = incapable
					}
					OR = {
						is_female = no
						trait = master_warrior
					}
					NOT = {
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							value = 0
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		create_random_soldier = {
			random_traits = yes
			dynasty = random
			female = no
			culture = ROOT
			religion = ROOT
		}
		new_character = {
			character_event = {
				id = lux_duels.1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB554350018"
		random = {
			chance = 75
 			add_trait = cynical
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = {
					id = 38258
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
	
#duel2
character_event = {
	id = 554350019
	desc = "EVTDESC554350019"
	picture = GFX_evt_royalcourt

    is_triggered_only = yes	
	
	only_playable = yes
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	ai = no

	trigger = {
			
		NOT = { has_character_flag = flavor_event_19 }	
		in_command = no
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				trait = on_hajj
				trait = stressed
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = flavor_event_19
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA554350019"
		set_character_flag = flag_duel_to_the_death
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		trigger = {
			any_courtier = {
				age = 16
				prisoner = no
				NOT = {
					trait = incapable
				}
				OR = {
					is_female = no
					trait = master_warrior
				}
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				age = 16
				prisoner = no
				NOT = {
					trait = incapable
				}
				OR = {
					is_female = no
					trait = master_warrior
				}
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = flag_duel_to_the_death
			character_event = {
				id = lux_duels.1
				tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPlux_duels.1"
			}
		}
	}

	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	ai = no

		num_traits = 7
		trait = stressed
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			num_traits = 8
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 6
			num_traits = 9
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA554350227"
		remove_trait = stressed
	}
}

## Random flavour/pop culture reference/whatever I come up with events. I'll eventually fill these out when I come up with more inspiration. - DarkReborn
# A strange priest from the east
character_event = {
	id = luxevents.1
	desc = "luxrandom.1"
	picture = "GFX_evt_zaratustra"
	border = "GFX_event_normal_frame_religion"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	ai = no

	trigger = {
		capital_scope = {
			OR = {
				empire = { title = e_scandinavia  }
				empire = { title = e_britannia }
				empire = { title = e_gallia }
				empire = { title = e_france }
				empire = { title = e_hre }
				empire = { title = e_spain }
				empire = { title = e_german }
				empire = { title = e_roman }
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				religion = indohelen
				religion_group = bud_group
				religion = mani
				religion = zoroastrian
				religion = indoh_zor
				religion = shaytana
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = { 
			days = 1
			modifier = { # Not as probable to happen
				factor = 0.5	
			}
			modifier = { # less than probable for the more isolated peoples 
				factor = 0.5
					capital_scope = {
						OR = {
							empire = { title = e_scandinavia  }
							empire = { title = e_britannia }
							empire = { title = e_german }
						}
					}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = mystic
			}
		}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAluxrandom.1 
		random_list = {
			20 = {
				create_character = {
					min_age = 20
					max_age = 60
					religion = indohelen
					culture = indohellenic
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					female = no
				}			
			}
			20 = {
				create_character = {
					min_age = 20
					max_age = 60
					religion = bud_pureland
					culture = tocharian
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					female = no
				}			
			}
			20 = {
				create_character = {
					min_age = 20
					max_age = 60
					religion = mani
					culture = uyghur
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					female = no
				}			
			}
			20 = {
				create_character = {
					min_age = 20
					max_age = 60
					religion = zoroastrian
					culture = persian
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					female = no
				}			
			}
			15 = { #THE strange eastern priestess
				create_character = { 
					name = Melisende
					min_age = 20
					max_age = 20
					religion = indoh_zor
					culture = tocharian
					attributes = {
						intrigue = 5 #The night is dark and full of terrors...
						learning = 5 #...but the fire burns them all the same.
					}
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					female = yes
				}
			}
			5 = { #PRAISE SHAYTANA INVICTUS
				create_character = {
					name = Shaytana
					min_age = 20
					max_age = 60
					attributes = {
						learning = 10 #for a whooping 20 learning
					}
					religion = shaytana
					culture = indohellenic
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					female = no
				}			
			}
		}
		new_character = {
			change_stewardship = 2
			change_intrigue = 4
			change_diplomacy = 4
			change_learning = 10
			ROOT = { religion = PREV }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBluxrandom.1
		piety = 25
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { trait = zealous } }
			random = {
				chance = 5
				add_trait = zealous
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 38269 }  }
			}
		}	
	}
		
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCluxrandom.1
		random_list = {
			20 = {
				create_character = {
					min_age = 20
					max_age = 60
					religion = indohelen
					culture = indohellenic
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					female = no
				}			
			}
			20 = {
				create_character = {
					min_age = 20
					max_age = 60
					religion = bud_pureland
					culture = tocharian
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					female = no
				}			
			}
			20 = {
				create_character = {
					min_age = 20
					max_age = 60
					religion = mani
					culture = uyghur
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					female = no
				}			
			}
			20 = {
				create_character = {
					min_age = 20
					max_age = 60
					religion = zoroastrian
					culture = persian
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					female = no
				}			
			}
			15 = { #THE strange eastern priestess
				create_character = { 
					name = Melisende #Approximate Greek of modern "Melissandre"... I guess.
					min_age = 20
					max_age = 30
					religion = indoh_zor
					culture = tocharian
					attributes = {
						intrigue = 5 #The night is dark and full of terrors...
						learning = 5 #...but the dawn burns them all the same.
					}
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					female = yes
				}
			}
			5 = { #PRAISE SHAYTANA INVICTUS
				create_character = {
					name = Shaytana
					min_age = 20
					max_age = 60
					learning = 10 #for a whooping 20 learning
					religion = shaytana
					culture = indohellenic
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					female = no
				}			
			}
		}
		new_character = {
			change_stewardship = 2
			change_intrigue = 4
			change_diplomacy = 4
			change_learning = 10
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { trait = cynical } 
				NOT = { trait = zealous } 
			}
			random = {
				chance = 15
				add_trait = cynical
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38258 #Notify Cynical
					}
				}
			}
		}		
	}
}

# Aztec scout
character_event = {
	id = luxevents.2
	desc = "luxrandom.2"
	picture = " GFX_evt_aztec_explorers"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	ai = no

	trigger = {
			has_dlc = "Sunset Invasion"
				#Cultures that have access to the Atlantic Ocean
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						empire = { title = e_scandinavia  }
						empire = { title = e_britannia }
						empire = { title = e_gallia }
						empire = { title = e_spain }
						kingdom = { title = k_mauretania }
						kingdom = { title = k_jolof }
					}
				}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = aztec_explorers } #No one has heard of the Aztecs yet...
	}

	weight_multiplier = { 
			days = 1
			modifier = { # Not as probable to happen
				factor = 0.5	
			}
			modifier = { # less probable for some too far away cultures
			factor = 0.5
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						empire = { title = e_scandinavia  }
						kingdom = { title = k_jolof }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.3
				trait = paranoid
			}
		}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAluxrandom.2 
		create_character = {
			min_age = 20
			max_age = 30
			religion = aztec
			culture = nahuatl
			random_traits = yes
			dynasty = random
			female = no
		}			
		new_character = {
			change_intrigue = 5
			change_diplomacy = 5
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBluxrandom.2

	trigger = { NOT = { trait = cynical } }
		prestige = 25
			create_character = {
				min_age = 20
				max_age = 30
				religion = aztec
				culture = nahuatl
				random_traits = yes
				dynasty = random
				female = no
			}			
			new_character = {
				imprison = ROOT
				change_intrigue = 5
				change_diplomacy = 5
			}
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { trait = paranoid } }
			random = {
				chance = 5
				add_trait = paranoid
			}
		}	
	}
		
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCluxrandom.2

	trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = lunatic
				trait = possessed
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			min_age = 20
			max_age = 30
			religion = aztec
			culture = nahuatl
			random_traits = yes
			dynasty = random
			female = no
		}			
		new_character = {
			ROOT = { religion = PREV }
			change_learning = 5
			change_diplomacy = 5
		}
	}
}

 # Travellers from far away lands
 #Germanic warrior
character_event = {
	id = luxevents.3
	desc = "EVTDESC3124150"
	picture = "GFX_evt_castle_rider_arriving"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	only_playable = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	ai = no

	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		prestige = 300
		wealth = 50
		higher_tier_than = baron
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				culture_group = north_germanic
				culture_group = central_germanic
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = traveller_received
			}
			had_character_flag = { flag = traveller_received days = 3650 }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			create_random_soldier = {
				random_traits = yes
				culture = visigothic
				dynasty = none
				female = no
				age = 30
			}
			new_character = {
				random_list = {
					25 = {
						culture = teutonic
						religion = german_pagan
					}
					25 = {
						culture = suevic
						religion = allfather
					}
					25 = {
						culture = vandal
						religion = arian
					}
					25 = {
						culture = visigothic
						religion = catholic
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					10 = { add_trait = duelist }
					10 = { add_trait = hunter }
					30 = { add_trait = trained_warrior }
					20 = { add_trait = skilled_warrior }
					10 = { add_trait = master_warrior }
					10 = {
						give_nickname = nick_the_traveller
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					20 = { add_trait = veteran }
					15 = { add_trait = honorable }
					15 = { add_trait = quick }
					15 = { add_trait = strong }
					10 = { add_trait = tolerant }
				}
				remove_trait = slow
				remove_trait = gluttonous
				remove_trait = arbitrary
				remove_trait = chaste
				remove_trait = craven
				remove_trait = slothful
				remove_trait = imbecile
				set_character_flag = arrived_traveller
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3124150"
		set_character_flag = traveller_received
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = arrived_traveller
			}
			clr_character_flag = arrived_traveller
		}
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB3124150"
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = arrived_traveller
			}
			banish = yes
			clr_character_flag = arrived_traveller
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC3124150"

	trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = cynical
				trait = shy
				trait = cruel
				trait = ruthless
				trait = deceitful
				intrigue = 12
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit ={
				NOT = {	trait = paranoid }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = paranoid
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = the_suspicious
			duration = 90
		}
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = arrived_traveller
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_execution
				killer = ROOT
			}
			clr_character_flag = arrived_traveller
		}
	}
}

## Altaic child's first horse flavour event chain
# Altaic child is now old enough for their first horse (Altaic culture group)
character_event = {
	id = lux_childhorses.700
	desc = "EVTDESCHORSES700"
	picture = GFX_evt_altaic_camp
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	min_age = 12
	max_age = 14
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

		NOT = { has_character_flag = flag_first_horse }
		culture_group = altaic
		liege = {
			culture_group = altaic
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			any_child = { character = ROOT }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAHORSES700"
		set_character_flag = flag_first_horse
		liege = { character_event = { id = lux_childhorses.701 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPHORSES701" } }
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = lux_childhorses.701
	desc = "EVTDESCHORSES701"
	picture = GFX_evt_altaic_camp
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# Only the wildest stallion will do
	option = {
		trigger = { wealth = 25 }
		name = "EVTOPTAHORSES701"
		wealth = -25
		FROM = { hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = lux_childhorses.702 } } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = content
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				FROM = { trait = strong }
				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				FROM = { trait = weak }
				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				FROM = { trait = brave }
				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				FROM = { trait = craven }
				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				FROM = { trait = dwarf }
				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				FROM = { trait = clubfooted }
				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				FROM = { trait = hunchback }
				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = { trait = ill }
				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				FROM = { trait = wounded }
				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				FROM = { trait = maimed }
				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				FROM = { is_female = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	
	# A gentle mare, easily ridden
	option = {
		trigger = { wealth = 25 }
		name = "EVTOPTBHORSES701"
		FROM = { hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = lux_childhorses.708 } } }
		wealth = -25
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
	}
	
	# A fleabitten nag
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTCHORSES701"
		FROM = {
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_mad_at_guardian months = 120 }
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = lux_childhorses.714 } }
		}
		prestige = -100
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = greedy
			}
		}
	}
}

namespace = lux_holytree
### The Sacred Tree flavour event chain (Western European Pagans)
# Priest Finds a Sacred Tree 
province_event = {
	id = lux_holytree.14
	desc = EVTDESCholytree.14
	picture = GFX_evt_skyrim_forest_celtic
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = allfather
			religion = celtic_pagan
			religion = dievas
			religion = endovellico
			religion = german_pagan
			religion = irminsul
			religion = lugh
			religion = peckols
			religion = perkunas
			religion = saule
			religion = teiwaz
		}
		owner = {
			OR = {
				religion = allfather
				religion = celtic_pagan
				religion = dievas
				religion = endovellico
				religion = german_pagan
				religion = irminsul
				religion = lugh
				religion = peckols
				religion = perkunas
				religion = saule
				religion = teiwaz
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			owner = {
				any_demesne_province = {
					has_province_modifier = holy_tree
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { religion = irminsul } #Special care for "holy trees"
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { learning = 21 } 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { learning = 18 } 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { learning = 15 } 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			owner = { NOT = { learning = 3 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			owner = { NOT = { learning = 6 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			owner = { NOT = { learning = 9 } }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAholytree.14
		owner = {
			piety = 50
			cash = -150
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = holy_tree
			duration = 3650
		}
		random_province_lord = {
			limit = {
				is_theocracy = yes
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_happy
				who = ROOT
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBholytree.14
		owner = {
			piety = -150
		}
		random_province_lord = {
			limit = {
				is_theocracy = yes
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_dislike
				who = ROOT
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = lux_holytree.15
	desc = EVTDESCholytree.15
	picture = GFX_evt_skyrim_forest_celtic
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_modifier = holy_tree
		OR = {
			religion = allfather
			religion = celtic_pagan
			religion = dievas
			religion = endovellico
			religion = german_pagan
			religion = irminsul
			religion = lugh
			religion = peckols
			religion = perkunas
			religion = saule
			religion = teiwaz
		}
		owner = {
			OR = {
				religion = allfather
				religion = celtic_pagan
				religion = dievas
				religion = endovellico
				religion = german_pagan
				religion = irminsul
				religion = lugh
				religion = peckols
				religion = perkunas
				religion = saule
				religion = teiwaz
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			owner = {
				has_character_modifier = pious_ruler
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAholytree.15
		owner = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = pious_ruler
				duration = 1200
			}
		}
		religion_authority = {
			modifier = holy_tree 
			years = 20
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = holy_tree
			duration = 365000
		}
	}
}
	
# Non-pagans destroy the tree
province_event = {
	id = lux_holytree.16
	desc = EVTDESCholytree.16
	picture = GFX_evt_skyrim_forest_celtic
	
	trigger = {
		any_realm_province = {
				has_province_modifier = holy_tree
			}
		owner = {
			NOT = { 			
				OR = {
					religion = allfather
					religion = celtic_pagan
					religion = dievas
					religion = endovellico
					religion = german_pagan
					religion = irminsul
					religion = lugh
					religion = peckols
					religion = perkunas
					religion = saule
					religion = teiwaz
				} 
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAholytree.16
		remove_province_modifier = holy_tree
		set_province_flag = destroyed_holy_tree
		owner = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = pious_ruler
				duration = 1200
			}
		}
		religion_authority = {
			modifier = destroyed_holy_tree 
			years = 20
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBholytree.16
		owner = {
			piety = -150
			}
	}
}
